       <script>
        for (var i = 0; i < menu_items_array.length; i++) {
                 var parent_node = menu_items_array[i].parentNode;
                 // Test and handle active menu item if page slug is 'image-gallery'
                 if ( window.location.href.indexOf('image-gallery') > -1 || window.location.href.indexOf('/case/') > -1 ) {
                     if (menu_items_array[i].innerText.toLowerCase() == "image library") {
                         jQuery(parent_node).addClass('current-menu-item');
                     }
                 }
                 // Hide mdpress menu item
                 if (menu_items_array[i].innerText.toLowerCase() == "discover platform" || menu_items_array[i].innerText.toLowerCase() == "discover beta") {
                     jQuery(parent_node).addClass('hidden');
                 }
             }
